
   *siyā **saṃkiliṭṭhasaṃkilesikā** dhammaṃ **paṭicca** **saṃkiliṭṭhasaṃkilesikā** dhammo uppajjeyya **na hetu piccayā**?

   *siyā **saṃkiliṭṭhasaṃkilesikā** dhammaṃ **paṭicca** **asaṃkiliṭṭhasaṃkilesikā** dhammo uppajjeyya **na hetu piccayā**?
